[38;2;255;255;255m⏺[39m [1mRoot Cause Analysis[22m

  [1mWhere the crash occurs:[22m
  - Line 26 in [38;2;177;185;249mdemo-buggy.c[39m, inside the [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m function
  - The crash happens when trying to access [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[s->num_scores][39m

  [1mWhy it crashes:[22m
  - [1mEXC_BAD_ACCESS (code=1, address=0x0)[22m - attempting to write to a NULL
  pointer
  - The [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m field in the Student struct is [38;2;177;185;249m0x0000000000000000[39m (NULL)
  - The program tries to dereference this NULL pointer to store a score
  value

  [1mRoot Cause:[22m
  The [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m array was never allocated memory. The Student struct was
  created with:
  - [38;2;177;185;249mname[39m: properly allocated and pointing to "Alice"
  - [38;2;177;185;249mage[39m: set to 20
  - [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m: NULL pointer (never allocated)
  - [38;2;177;185;249mnum_scores[39m: 0

  When [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m tries to write to [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[0][39m, it's attempting to write
   to memory address 0x0, which causes a segmentation fault.

  [1mCall Stack:[22m
  1. [38;2;177;185;249mmain()[39m at line 56 calls [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m
  2. [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m crashes at line 26 when dereferencing the NULL [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m
  pointer

  [1mFix Required:[22m
  The [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m array needs to be allocated memory (e.g., using [38;2;177;185;249mmalloc()[39m)
  before attempting to store score values.
